   <script type="text/javascript">
    if (window.location.href.indexOf('detailcruise')<0) { //no need on background pages
 
     	var loadExtrasMenu = function(url) {
 
     		var data = [];
     		$.ajax({
     			type: "GET",
     			url: url,
     			dataType: "json",
     			async: true,
     			success: drawExtras
     		})
 
     	}
 
     	var drawExtras = function(results) {
         
     		if (results.success != 1) return false;
     		var con = $("#SpecialOffers_menu .menu-panel > ul");
 
         var tpl = "<li><a href='/deals.phtml?id={{id}}&{{stub}}' class='menu-item foco-headline'>{{val}} <span class='raquo'>»</span></a></li>";
     		
     		$(results.response).each(function() {
 					var stub = this.cruises.val.replace(/[\W_]+/g,"-");
     			var html = tpl.replace(/{{id}}/g, this.cruises.rule_id);
 	        html = html.replace(/{{val}}/g, this.cruises.val);
           html = html.replace(/{{stub}}/g, stub);
         
     			con.append(html);
     		});
     	}
 
 
     	$(document).ready(loadExtrasMenu("//api.virginholidayscruises.co.uk/Products/menuExtras/"));
     }
   </script>

   <link href="https://static.traveltek.net/images/www.virginholidayscruises.co.uk/js/jquery.countdown.package-2.0.1/jquery.countdown.css?1" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"/>
   <link href="https://static.traveltek.net/images/www.virginholidayscruises.co.uk/js/jquery.countdown.package-2.0.1/custom-countdown.rb.css?1" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"/>

   <div class="sixteen columns" id="countdown_banner">
    <div>
     <div class="bigText_block columns rotating-panel">
     </div>
     <div class="timer_block four columns rotating-panel active-tile">
      <div id="countdownStart">
      </div>
      <div id="countdownEnd">

   <script>
    ( function($) {
 $(document).ready(function() {	
 
         //Master Switch
         var bannerOpts = {"show":"timed"};
 	
 	//Countdown Dates NOTE: Jan:0, Feb:1, Mar:2 etc
 	var countStart = new Date(2018, 4, 25, 0, 0, 0 ,1);   //Set START date	
 	var countEnd = new Date(2018, 4, 28, 23, 59, 59, 0);   //Set END date	
 	
 	//Banner Copy Variables
 	var bigText = 'SAVE UP TO 10%';
 	var halfText = '';
 	var timerMsg = '';
 	
 	//Banner Link
 	var banner_link = '/sale';
 	
 	//Date Formatting
 	var dayFormat = ['SUNDAY','MONDAY','TUESDAY','WEDNESDAY','THURSDAY','FRIDAY','SATURDAY'];
 	var monthFormat = ['JANUARY','FEBRUARY','MARCH','APRIL','MAY','JUNE','JULY', 'AUGUST','SEPTEMBER', 'OCTOBER','NOVEMBER','DECEMBER'];
 	
 	var bannerDay = dayFormat[countEnd.getDay()];
 	var bannerDate = countEnd.getDate();
         var bannerMonth = monthFormat[countEnd.getMonth()];
 
 
 	var items = $(".rotating-panel");
 	var length = items.length;
 	var index = 0;
 	var active_class_name = "active-tile";
 
 	
 	setInterval(function() {
 
 		if (index>(length-1)) index = 0;
 		$("."+active_class_name).removeClass(active_class_name);
 		items.eq(index).addClass(active_class_name);
 		index++;
 	}, 3*1000);
 	
 
 		
 	function nth(d) {
 	if(d>3 && d<21) return 'TH';
 		switch (d % 10){
 			case 1: return 'ST';
 			case 2: return 'ND';
 			case 3: return 'RD';
 			default: return 'TH';
 		}
 	}
 	
 	var fullDateBanner = bannerDay + ' ' + bannerDate+nth(bannerDate)  + ' ' +  bannerMonth;
 	
 	
 	
 	//Start Count
 	$('#countdownStart').countdown({until: countStart, onExpiry: bannerStart, alwaysExpire: true, layout: '<div><span>{dn}</span>Days</div><div><span>{hn}</span>{hl}</div><div><span>{mn}</span>{ml}</div><div><span>{sn}</span>{sl}</div>'}).hide();
 	
 	//End count
        var countEndPlus = new Date(countEnd.setDate(countEnd.getDate() +1));
        var countEndPlus = new Date();
        countEndPlus.setTime(countEnd.getTime());
 
 
 	$('#countdownEnd').countdown({until: countEndPlus, onExpiry: bannerEnd, alwaysExpire: true, layout: '<div><span>{dn}</span>Days</div><div><span>{hn}</span>Hrs</div><div><span>{mn}</span>Mins</div><div><span>{sn}</span>Secs</div>'}).hide();
 	
 	//Day Before Count
 //	var count24 = new Date(countEnd.setDate(countEnd.getDate() -1));
 
 	var count24 = new Date(); //BF - adjusted to include time
 	count24.setTime(countEnd.getTime() - (1000*60*60*24));
 
 	$('#countdown24').countdown({until: count24, onExpiry: bannerEnd, alwaysExpire: true, layout: '<div><span>{dn}</span>Days</div><div><span>{hn}</span>Hrs</div><div><span>{mn}</span>Mins</div><div><span>{sn}</span>Secs</div>'}); //.hide();
 	
 
 
 	//Banner Copy
 	function CountdownCopy(a,b,c,d){
 		$('.bigText_block').text(a);
 		$('.halfText_block').text(b);
 		$('.timer_msg').text(c);
 		$('#fullDate').text(d);
 	}
 	
 	//Banner Link
 	$('#countdown_banner').click(function(){
 		window.open(banner_link, "_self");
 	});
 	
 	//$('.banner-btn').attr("href", banner_link );
 	
 	
 	function bannerStart() { 
 		$('#countdown_banner').css('display','block');
                 //$('#countdown_banner').attr('style','display:block');
 	}
 	
 	function lessThan24() { 
 		$('#countdownEnd').css('display','block');
 		$('#countdown24, #fullDate').hide();
 	}
 	
 	function bannerEnd() { 
 		$('#countdown_banner').css('display','none');
 	}
 	
 	
 	CountdownCopy( bigText, halfText, timerMsg, fullDateBanner );
 
         
         //Master Switch
         var bannerChoice = bannerOpts.show;
 
         switch (bannerChoice){
     
           case 'true':
             $('#countdown_banner').css('display','block');
             break;
     
           case 'false':
             $('#countdown_banner').css('display','none');
             break;
 
           case 'timed':
             return;
             break;
 
           default: 
             return;
  
         }
 
 	
 });
 } ) ( jQuery );
   </script>

     <script language="Javascript">
      var typevals = document.getElementById("type-api");
 var type = typevals.options[typevals.selectedIndex].text;
 
 var regionvals = document.getElementById("regionid-api");
 var region = regionvals.options[regionvals.selectedIndex].text;
 
 var linevals = document.getElementById("lineid-api");
 var line = linevals.options[linevals.selectedIndex].text;
 
 var deptdateval = $("#search-datepicker").val();
 
 if(deptdateval=="") {
 var deptmonthyear = "Any Departure Date";
 }
 else {
 var deptdatearray = deptdateval.split("-");
 var deptmonthyear = deptdatearray[2] + "-" + deptdatearray[1];
 }
 
 var trackingstring = type + " | " + region + " | " + line + " | " + deptmonthyear
 
 
 function searchtracking() {
 
 
 	//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Forms', 'Search Submit', trackingstring]);
 	ga('send', 'event', {
 		'eventCategory': "Search Form",
 		'eventAction': "Submit",
 		'eventLabel': trackingstring,
 		'nonInteraction': false
 	});
 
 
 	}
     </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      function setform() {
 var thispage = document.URL;
 
 
 setfield("lineid", "");		
 setfield("shipid", "");
 setfield("regionid", "");
 setfield("systemgroup", "");
 
 
 
 
 // departure and return dates for trailfinders cruise
 setfield("depdate-year", "2018");
 
 if ( document.getElementById('depdate-month') ) {
 	var regex = /^0/;
 	var depmonth = document.getElementById('depdate-month').value;
 	
 	if (!depmonth) {
 		var opts = [];		
 		var month = document.getElementById("depdate-month");
 		
 		for (i = 0; i < month.options.length; i++) {
 			opts.push(month.options[i].value);
 		}
 		
 		if ( opts[0] == "01" || opts[1] == "01" ) {
 			setfield("depdate-month", "06");
 		}
 	} else {
 		if ( depmonth.toString().match(regex) ) {
 			setfield("depdate-month", "06");
 		} else {
 			var tochange = "06";
 	 		var dep = tochange.replace(regex, "");
 	 		setfield("depdate-month", dep);
 		}
 	}
 }
 
 setfield("depdate-day", "27");
 setfield("depdatefull", "27/06/2018");
 setfield("depdateiso", "2018-06-27");
 setfield("depdate-monthyear", "06_2018");
 
 setfield("retdate-year", "2018");
 
 if ( document.getElementById('retdate-month') ) {
 	var regex = /^0/;
 	var retmonth = document.getElementById('retdate-month').value;
 	
 	if (!retmonth) {
 		var opts = [];		
 		var month = document.getElementById('depdate-month');
 		
 		for (i = 0; i < month.options.length; i++) {
 			opts.push(month.options[i].value);
 		}
 		
 		if ( opts[0] == "01" || opts[1] == "01" ) {
 			setfield("retdate-month", "07");
 		}
 		
 	} else {
 		if ( retmonth.toString().match(regex) ) {
 			setfield("retdate-month", "07");
 		} else {
 	 		var tochange = "07";
 	 		var ret = tochange.replace(regex, "");
 	 		setfield("retdate-month", ret);
 		}
 	}
 }
 
 setfield("retdate-day", "4");
 setfield("retdatefull", "04/07/2018");
 setfield("retdateiso", "2018-07-04");
 
 setfield("day", "");
 setfield("monthyear", "06_2018");		
 setfield("daysplusminus", "");
 setfield("startport", "");		
 setfield("port", "");
 setfield("endport", "");
 setfield("homecity", "");
 setfield("adults", "2");		
 setfield("children", "");
 setfield("infants", "");
 setfield("lowestavailablefare", "");
 setfield("military", "");
 setfield("includesenior", "");
 setfield("pastpassenger", "");
 setfield("filterprice", "");
 setfield("spreadnights", "");
 setfield("departuk", "");
 setfield("cruiseonly", "");
 setfield("depair", "CO");
 setfield("flycruise", "");
 setfield("nofly", "");
 setfield("classificationid", "");
 setfield("supplierpromocode", "");
 
 setfield("keyword", "");
 setfield("extraid", "");
 setfield("maxseadays", "");
 setfield("groupid", "");
 
 if ('' != '' && !document.getElementById('branch').disabled) {
 	setfield("branch", "");
 	if ('' != '' && $('branch')) {
 		updatebranchusers('');
 	}
 	setfield("bookinguser", "");
 	setfield("team", "");	
 }
 
 
 
 
 cruiseformjs();
 //connections.update("line");
 
 
 }
 setform();
     </script>

           <img alt="" border="0" id="" orgheight="397" orgwidth="680" src="https://static.traveltek.net/uploaded/2017/5/1494869235.jpg" usemap="#map"/>
           <script type="text/javascript">
            ( function($) {
 
   var setImageMap = function() {
     var w = $(window).width();
     var w_threshold = 765;
     if (w>w_threshold) enableMap();
     else disableMap();
   }
 
   var enableMap = function() {
     $("map").unbind("click").css("cursor", "pointer");
     $("area").unbind("click").css("cursor", "pointer");
   }
 
   var disableMap = function() {
     $("map").click(function() {
       return false;
     }).css("cursor", "default");
     $("area").click(function() {
       return false;
     }).css("cursor", "default");
   }
 
   $(window).resize(setImageMap);
 
   $(window).ready(function() {
   	setImageMap();
   });
 
 } ) ( jQuery );
           </script>
